        logger.info('logged in as: '+conn.getUser());          // set the presence status         presence = new Presence(Presence.Type.available);         logger.info('Set presence as: '+Presence.Type.available);         conn.sendPacket(presence);     } /* login */       public void createChatListener(){         GtalkMessageListener msgListener = new GtalkMessageListener();         //PacketFilter filter = new MessageTypeFilter(Message.Type.chat);         PacketFilter filter = new PacketTypeFilter(Message.class);         conn.addPacketListener(msgListener, filter);     } /* createChatListener */       public void incrementalNap(){         if(sleepCount < MAX_SLEEP_COUNT){             sleepSec = sleepSec << 1;         }     } /*  incrementalNap */  } </code></pre>  <p>Thanks in advance, guys.</p>
